### [276] [Twitter climate discourse as a signal of pro-environmental behaviors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27330)
*Edoardo Maggioni,Diego Garlaschelli,Rossana Mastrandrea,Luca Maria Aiello*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本研究结合Twitter地理定位数据与欧洲晴雨表调查数据，发现欧洲地区气候相关推文密度与亲环境行为呈正相关，但不同类型在线话语（如行动主义和社会支持表达）与线下行为呈负相关，表明在线气候话语可作为区域亲环境行为的注意力信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模协调的亲环境行为对气候减缓至关重要，但传统调查工具难以监测个体行为的广泛扩散与社会协调过程，因此需要探索新的数据源来捕捉这一动态。

Method: 结合2017-2019年地理定位Twitter数据（气候变化推特数据集）与2019年特别欧洲晴雨表调查数据，以欧洲地区为分析单元，计算气候推文密度与自我报告亲环境行为数量的关联，并使用NLP工具分解在线话语的社会维度（知识交流、行动主义、社会支持）。

Result: 推文密度与亲环境行为呈强正相关，该结果在社会经济控制变量、替代空间聚合和多种稳健性检验下依然稳健。知识交流与线下行为无显著关联，而行动主义和社会支持相关表达与亲环境行为呈负相关。

Conclusion: 在线气候话语可作为区域亲环境行为差异的注意力信号，但不同形式的在线参与与线下行为的关系存在显著差异。研究展示了将大规模数字痕迹与调查数据整合以研究社会-环境系统中集体行为的潜力，同时保持观察性研究视角。

Abstract: Fostering coordinated pro-environmental behaviors at scale is a key challenge for climate mitigation. Individual actions only generate meaningful impact when they diffuse widely and become socially coordinated, yet monitoring such processes remains difficult with traditional survey-based tools alone.
  In this study, we examine whether large-scale online climate discourse is associated with differences in offline pro-environmental behavior across European regions. We combine geolocated Twitter data from the Climate Change Twitter Dataset (2017-2019) with survey-based measures from the 2019 Special Eurobarometer, focusing on the regional density of climate-related tweets and the average number of self-reported pro-environmental actions.
  We find a strong positive association between tweet density and pro-environmental behavior that remains robust to socio-economic controls, alternative spatial aggregations, and a wide range of robustness checks. To move beyond aggregate volume, we further decompose online discourse using Natural Language Processing tools that capture distinct social dimensions. While knowledge exchange shows no clear relationship with offline behavior, the prevalence of activism- and social support-related expressions is negatively associated with pro-environmental actions.
  Overall, our results suggest that online climate discourse can serve as an informative, attention-related signal of regional differences in pro-environmental behavior, but that different forms of online engagement relate to offline action in markedly different ways. More broadly, the study highlights the potential of integrating large-scale digital traces with survey data to investigate collective behavior in socio-environmental systems, while remaining explicitly observational in scope.

</details>


### [277] [From Notepad AI to Social Media: How Can Text Style Transformation Mitigate Social Harm?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27365)
*Syed Mhamudul Hasan,Mohd. Farhan Israk Soumik,Abdur R. Shahid*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个写作辅助框架，通过风格化文本转换（而非删除或审查）将攻击性、毒性评论转化为更中性温和的表达，同时保留语义核心信息，并引入情感漂移指数（EDI）量化评估改写效果，以减少在线环境中的有害互动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内容审核大多聚焦于检测和删除有害帖子，但较少关注通过保留语义的同时进行风格化文本转换来减轻伤害，这促使作者探索一种更柔和的替代方案。

Method: 提出一个写作辅助框架，借鉴Notepad AI的思路，对攻击性、毒性或情感有害的评论进行受控的风格化改写，使其变为更柔和、中性的表达形式；同时引入情感漂移指数（EDI）指标来系统量化情感变化并评估改写效果。

Result: 该方法能够在保留核心信息的前提下降低情感强度和基于身份的攻击性，从而减少有害互动。

Conclusion: 通过风格化文本转换而非直接审查，可以在不压制言论自由的前提下有效减轻社交媒体上的内容伤害，EDI指标为评估这类方法提供了定量工具。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of harmful and emotionally damaging content on social media platforms has intensified concerns regarding societal harm. While content moderation efforts primarily focus on detecting and removing harmful posts, less attention has been given to mitigating harm through stylistic text transformation while preserving semantic meaning. In this paper, we propose a writing-assistance framework that can reduce societal harm by transforming aggressive, toxic, or emotionally harmful comments into softer, more neutral stylistic forms inspired by Notepad AI, a simple AI writing assistant. Rather than censoring or suppressing speech, we apply controlled stylistic modifications to preserve core informational content while reducing emotional intensity and identity-based attacks. We introduce an Emotion Drift Index (EDI) metric to systematically quantify emotional change and evaluate the effectiveness of stylistic rewriting, thereby reducing harmful interactions in online environments.

</details>


### [278] [Gender Bias in YouTube Exposure: Allocative and Structural Inequalities in Political Information Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27479)
*Jipeng Tan,Weifeng Zhang,Ye Wu,Jialin Guo,Yong Min*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文以YouTube为案例，通过受控社交机器人实地实验，发现男性编码与女性编码档案在推荐系统中存在显著的政治信息分配偏差（议题分布、意识形态倾向、政治实体）和结构性偏差（社区聚类模式），并通过协同过滤模型复现了这些性别偏差，揭示了推荐系统不仅分配政治内容不均，而且通过社区结构强化社会不平等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐算法已成为数字平台信息分配的主导机制，但其中的性别偏差可能导致用户在不同政治信息环境中获得不平等的内容曝光。现有研究对推荐系统中性别偏差如何影响政治信息的分配与结构尚不充分，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用受控社交机器人实地实验，构建男性编码和女性编码的用户档案，在YouTube平台上追踪推荐轨迹和点击模式。从分配偏差（议题分布、意识形态取向、政治实体）和结构性偏差（社区聚类模式）两个维度分析推荐内容，并构建协同过滤模型复现观察到的性别偏差。

Result: 1) 男性编码与女性编码档案在分配偏差上存在统计显著差异，尤其在议题分布、意识形态取向和政治实体方面；2) 政治信息环境中存在结构性偏差，表现为不同的聚类模式；3) 时间序列分析显示，共现网络中的社区与个体档案层面的动态共同塑造了曝光路径。

Conclusion: 推荐系统中的性别偏差不仅体现在政治内容的分配不均，还通过社区结构塑造信息环境，从而强化社会不平等。这凸显了算法公平性的重要性。

Abstract: Recommendation algorithms have become the dominant mechanism for information distribution on digital platforms, profoundly shaping personalized information consumption environments. However, gender bias, as a significant form of algorithmic discrimination, may cause users to experience unequal exposure within different political information environments. Taking YouTube as a case, we conduct a controlled social-bot field experiment, where male-coded and female-coded profiles are constructed. We track the exposure and click patterns of these bots to analyze their recommendation trajectories. We analyze the distribution of recommended content from two dimensions: allocative bias and structural bias. First, we find statistically significant differences in allocative bias across male-coded and female-coded profiles, particularly in terms of issue distribution, ideological orientation, and political entities. Secondly, we observe structural bias in the political information environments, characterized by distinct clustering patterns. Additionally, time-series analysis shows that exposure pathways continue to be shaped over time by both communities detected in the co-occurrence network and individual profile-level dynamics. Finally, we construct a simple collaborative-filtering model that reproduces the observed gender bias. We argue that gender bias in recommendation systems is reflected not only in the allocation of political content, but also in how community structures shape these environments, reinforcing societal inequalities and highlighting the need for algorithmic fairness.

</details>


### [279] [Temporal and Content Coupling Analysis of Social Media User Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27530)
*Jipeng Tan,Mengye Yang,Zhanghao Li,Yong Min*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本研究提出一个多尺度时间-内容框架，在MIND和Adressa两个大型新闻数据集上，揭示了从宏观昼夜节律、中观幂律分布到微观指数分布的分层时间模式，并发现用户点击行为主要由历史兴趣驱动，但这种依赖随内容多样性增加而减弱；时间-内容耦合表明历史兴趣主导活跃时段的行为，且不同偏好群体（时效性、娱乐性、多样性）在点击频率和内容敏感性上存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对新闻消费行为中时间动态与内容选择之间的耦合机制理解不足，缺乏一个统一的多尺度分析框架来揭示不同时间层次上的行为模式及其与内容特征的交互作用。

Method: 提出多尺度时间-内容框架：宏观尺度使用傅里叶建模识别昼夜节律；中观尺度分析会话间隔的幂律分布；微观尺度建模会话内动作计数和间隔的指数分布。同时进行内容分析（历史兴趣、内容多样性）和时间-内容耦合分析。

Result: 成功识别出三层时间模式：宏观昼夜节律、中观幂律分布（α≈1）、微观指数分布（λ≈0.3和λ≈0.02）；点击主要由历史兴趣驱动，且该依赖随内容多样性增加而减弱；时间-内容耦合表明历史兴趣主导活跃时段；不同偏好群体（时效性、娱乐性、多样性）在行为模式上存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 新闻消费行为呈现分层时间结构，用户的历史兴趣与内容多样性之间存在动态权衡，偏好群体差异显著，这为个性化新闻推荐系统提供了理论依据和设计启示。

Abstract: News consumption behavior is shaped by the coupling between temporal dynamics and content selection. This study proposes a multi-scale temporal-content framework and validates it on two large real-world news datasets, MIND and Adressa. Results reveal hierarchical temporal patterns. At the macroscale, Fourier modeling identifies clear circadian rhythms; at the mesoscale, session intervals follow a power-law distribution with $α\approx 1$; and at the microscale, within-session action counts and inter-action intervals follow exponential distributions with $λ\approx 0.3$ and $λ\approx 0.02$, respectively. Content analysis shows that clicks are mainly driven by historical interests, while this dependence weakens as content diversity increases. Temporal-content coupling further indicates that users' historical interests dominate active time periods in shaping behavior. Preference groups also differ: timeliness and entertainment-oriented users click more frequently and rely more on historical interests, whereas diversified users click less and are more sensitive to content diversity.

</details>


### [280] [Social Media Data Toolkit: Standardization and Anonymization of Social Network Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27710)
*Ali Najafi,Letizia Iannucci,Mikko Kivelä,Onur Varol*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Social Media Data Toolkit (SMDT)，一个用于标准化、匿名化和丰富社交网络数据集的 Python 框架，旨在解决跨平台社交媒体分析中的数据异构问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体平台日益多样化，官方 API 限制增加，导致跨平台分析面临数据异构、结构不一致等挑战。研究者需要回答平台异同、数据采集方式、如何对齐数据集三个关键问题。

Method: SMDT 框架将不同数据源统一为通用模式（包含 Communities、Accounts、Posts、Actions、Entities），提供可配置的匿名化模块保护 PII，并集成 LLM 和网络分析工具的可扩展富化层，支持下游任务如立场检测和毒性评分。

Result: 通过四个案例研究（涵盖文本分析和网络分析）展示了 SMDT 的多功能性，证明其能在不同平台上进行公平分析，无需为不同数据集单独编写代码。

Conclusion: SMDT 作为开源工具发布，提供详细文档和实践指南，可促进可复现的社交媒体研究，降低跨平台分析的技术门槛。

Abstract: The rapid diversification of social media platforms and the increasing restrictions on official APIs have significantly complicated cross-platform analysis. Researchers are often forced to rely on heterogeneous datasets obtained through web scraping and historical archives; however they often lack structural consistency. Prior to conducting cross-platform social media analyses, one needs to answer three critical questions: (1) What makes platforms different and similar? (2) How were the datasets collected? (3) How can we align the datasets of different platforms to conduct fair analyses? To address these questions, we introduce the Social Media Data Toolkit (\projectname{}), a comprehensive Python framework designed for the standardization, anonymization, and enrichment of social network datasets. \projectname{} unifies diverse data structures into a generic schema comprising Communities, Accounts, Posts, Actions, and Entities to facilitate multi-platform research. The framework features a configurable anonymization module to secure Personally Identifiable Information (PII) and an extendable enrichment layer that integrates Large Language Models (LLMs) and network analysis tools for downstream tasks such as stance detection and toxicity scoring without creating codebase for different datasets. We demonstrate the versatility of \projectname{} through four case studies spanning from textual analysis of the content to network analysis across platforms. To offer reproducible social media research, \projectname{} is released as an open-source tool featuring detailed documentation and practical guides for researchers at any skill-level. It can be accessed at github.com/ViralLab/SMDT and varollab.com/SMDT.

</details>
